2/6/24, 11:06â€¯PM - Shibajyoti KIIT: Dear Sir/Ma'am ,  I hope this email finds you well. I am writing to bring to your attention an issue regarding the current availability of weights, plates, and barbells in the college gym of Campus 15. 

 As an active participant in the gym, I have noticed that the current inventory of these essential equipment is insufficient to accommodate the growing number of students utilizing the facilities. This shortage often leads to long waiting times and inconvenience for those trying to complete their workouts effectively.  

In order to ensure that all students have access to a fully equipped gym and to promote a healthy and active lifestyle on campus, I kindly request that additional weights, plates, and barbells be provided.We need dumbbells of weight 25kg , 30kg and 35kg atleast as the maximum dumbbell weight is 50pounds (22.6kg) which is not sufficient for workout. We also need more plates of 15kg , 25kg and also deadlift and bench press barbells.

Increasing the availability of these resources would not only enhance the overall experience for gym-goers but also contribute to the physical well-being of the student body as a whole.

I understand that budgetary constraints may be a consideration, but I believe that investing in the expansion of our gym equipment would be a worthwhile investment in the health and fitness of our student community.

Thank you for considering this request. I look forward to hearing from you regarding any updates or developments on this matter.

Best regards,
Shibajyoti Choudhury
